1)
Words for the 15th Parents' Day
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Today, March 24, 1974, lunar March 1, we are holding the 15th Parents' Day celebration at this center in Jackson, the central city of Mississippi. This is the time of the 14th year, the last year of the second 7-year course. 
Father, I sincerely thank You for expanding the foundation of providential victory through the fierce struggles of the members in Korea, extending spiritual expectations from national standards to global expectations, allowing us to hold such a gathering on this American land today. 
Father, I thank You for leading us to fulfill the sorrowful heart You have carried for humanity since the day of the Fall, enabling us to resolve Your grief. 
Now, we must connect this spiritual foundation to a tangible foundation, as a small, transcultural group of unity on earth. Father, we truly recognize that it is through Your hard work and efforts that we have been able to fight for the past three years. 
Father, I sincerely thank You for allowing us to hold this gathering of hope on this day, as we advance toward 40 cities in the final year of the 3-year course in this land of America, and for enabling us to celebrate the 15th Parents' Day here. 
March 24, 1974 (Sun), Jackson Church (Mississippi, USA).
* These words were spoken on the 15th Parents' Day, and the title was added by the editor.
8   Words for the 15th Parents' Day
May all the connections and relationships involved in this journey You are moving forward be bound for Your will. May the resurrection of Your life arise in the hearts of countless people who have heard Your words, so that they cannot forget and will surely seek refuge in Your embrace, mobilizing good ancestors to connect them. 
Furthermore, among the countless saints in heaven and the many religious leaders who have come and gone on this earth, may the spiritual world be organized around Jesus, Confucius, Buddha, and Muhammad. Thus, centered on Jesus, the True Parents' family, the True Parents' nation, the True Parents' world, may we proclaim this year that we must advance toward the unified universe You desire, expanding their activity stage, and allow the good people who sacrificed their lives for their denominations to be gathered into one purpose, so that the nations, tribes, and clans on earth may be drawn into a unified destiny. Please allow the spiritual front of unity to unfold over all humanity. Additionally, may the good kings and loyal subjects centered on each nation, and all spirits who have sacrificed for their nations, be gathered here. May this intention be supported wherever it goes. 
Especially, Father, mobilize the good kings and patriots in Korea, and unite those who have worked for the Unification Church and have gone to the spiritual world, to protect and completely safeguard the path of the Parents. Please allow the time to come when we can open the final front and resolve historical grievances. 
When I think of the second 7-year course set for April, I earnestly hope and wish that this period will become a new historical turning point. 
And may the special love of the Father be present wherever the members in East Garden, Belvedere, or in Korea, Japan, and the United States offer prayers and worship during this time. I earnestly hope and wish that this day will be a day to praise the glory of victory. 
Through this gathering, Father, I sincerely hope and wish it will become an opportunity to elevate the prayer for the victory of a new nation and to uplift Your will. 
As we celebrate the 15th Parents' Day, may the heart of reverence for parents grow even stronger as the years go by. As we advance toward the world in the third 7-year course after this year, I earnestly hope and wish that we may be blessed to praise Your glory based on the authority of the restoration of the spirit and body for nations and the world. 
Please bless this day. May everything that commemorates and celebrates this day bring joy and glory, bringing liberation before all people, and may the time of heaven unfold where good and evil can distinguish themselves and the opposing forces of good and evil can comply with the original foundation. I earnestly hope and wish for this. 
I offer all the pure hearts before You, Father, so please do not leave any shortcomings as conditions, and allow anything to become a condition for Your praise. I earnestly ask and wish for this. 
I completely entrust this year to You, Father. I earnestly ask and wish that the remaining 7-year course, as we advance toward the third course, may be filled with infinite blessings and the flag of victory may be raised high in the cosmos. I earnestly ask and wish that our transcultural movement may advance on a global foundation. 
I earnestly ask and wish that this day may be a source of pride. May glory and love be with us forever in all matters, and may it be fulfilled within Your will, I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
<Words> As you all know, today is 'Parents' Day.' In terms of cycles, it is the 14th cycle, and in terms of counts, it is the 15th time. 
After proclaiming the 7-year course in 1960, the first 7-year course and the second 7-year course will conclude this year. 
Now, centered on the third 7-year course, we will enter the global restoration period until 1981. 
10   Words for the 15th Parents' Day
The significance of the victory of the 3-year course in America, representing the democratic world
As you all know, these three years in America… This is not just a preparation for the next three years after completing the second 7-year course. The period of the 3-year course before the end of the second 7-year course is a preparation period to advance toward the global 7-year course. You must understand that this period is a preparation for the full-scale commencement of the global 7-year course based on the 3-year course of the second 7-year course. 
This position is comparable to the spiritual standard that Jesus represented in establishing a nation of the Jews and connecting it to a nation of Rome. 
So what is the difference between the time of Jesus and now? The time of Jesus was a national era, but now is a global era. There is such a difference. Therefore, laying this foundation in America, which represents the democratic world, centered on the 3-year course, has historical significance for victory. 
In contrast, what is the country that stands as the enemy of the democratic world? If we see this democratic world as Abel, then the country that stands as Cain is the communist world. 
Now, if we can affirm the results of victory in the second 7-year course in America and just get through this 3-year course, the global satanic world will inevitably enter a stage where it must retreat in terms of spiritual standards. 
Establishing a tangible foundation in America during the third 7-year course
So what is our current position? Centered on America, while the teacher is laying this foundation here, the communist world has a basis that can substitute for the tangible foundation, while we still do not possess that foundation. Therefore, you must understand that the communists are standing in opposition to us, pushing for the preparation of the foundation that you do not know about. If we look at this democratic world like Abel, it is like separating the spirit and the flesh. As we occupy the spiritual aspect, the physical foundation must also be related to it, and we must go out in an opposing position to ensure that we can achieve victory and occupy everything. 
From this perspective, the period from 1972 to 1978 will be a time of division both internally and externally, and a time when we confront each other. You must understand that this fight is how we will complete the history of 7,000 years into one America during this 7-year period. 
When I mentioned last year and during the public lectures in 1972 that the greatest crisis in America would be in 1977 and 1978, it was based on this principle. Therefore, now, during this 1974 'Day of Hope' tour, it concludes that there must be communist manipulation behind those who actively oppose us. Groups like Jesus People and Jesus Freaks must have communist involvement. The continuous opposition from the New York gathering nationwide comes from such motivations, viewed providentially. Now, in the Christian position, there are factions that oppose us and factions that support us, but they are ultimately leaning toward opposition. 
Why is that? If we regard the communists as a revival stage, they have established a middle form of historical growth, which is comparable to the time of Jesus. Therefore, Christianity will inevitably oppose us just as Judaism opposed Jesus in His time. 
From a principled perspective, the revival stage and the growth stage are under the dominion of Satan, and heaven is preparing the completion stage. Since we are in the position of the completion stage, there will be opposition from the revival and growth stages, but since we have the foundation of the completion stage, the time has come when we can transcend the global foundation. When we completely transcend the nation and become one powerfully, Satan will retreat. This is the principle of the principled view. The revival and growth stages can be manipulated by Satan, but when we enter the completion stage, Satan cannot act freely. You must understand that we have entered such a position. 
From this standpoint, we are in the position of having entered the completion stage, so we cannot have national sentiments, clan sentiments, or feelings of discrimination among humanity. Now, since God has established a spiritual foundation for unity directly under His authority, we are completely united here. 
Now, from this perspective, you all have only one heart. Do not have any other thoughts. Just as Adam and Eve fell when they thought of themselves and sought to elevate themselves, you too have the potential to fall. Thinking of yourself can lead to your downfall. 
From this perspective, what attitude should Adam and Eve have had at that time? They should have always thought of God, and then of God's beloved sons and daughters, and God's beloved family, and this expectation of the son-in-law. They should not have thought of anything else. 
But what position are you in now? The old Adam and Eve only had spiritual Satan, but we have both spiritual and tangible Satan. You must understand that we have both spiritual Satan and tangible Satan. Therefore, mere determination is not enough. We have a messianic mission to save the fallen world. In other words, we must save our ancestors. We must save our ancestors in the spiritual world, save the tribes on this earth, and then we have the responsibility to save our own families. Spiritually speaking, one person is like a nation. 
Do you understand what I mean? It works in reverse. If you look here, your ancestors are in the spiritual world, and in the tangible world, you have your clan and family. This is how your origin exists. 
What happened with the fall of Adam and Eve? As a result of the fall of Adam and Eve, they destroyed the angelic world and the world of Adam. Then, they destroyed God's family. 
Therefore, this must be restored through indemnity, but to restore my family… 
13 
I cannot restore just my family. The Old Testament era, the New Testament era, and the Completed Testament era mean that the Old Testament era is the angelic world, the New Testament era is the tangible world of the time of Jesus, and the Completed Testament era is the era centered on families, centered on the True Parents. That is why today our Unification Church does not tolerate those who think of themselves. This is the time we are in. 
Democracy as a means to replace the side of Satan with the side of Heaven
Until now, what kind of war has God been waging? It is like conducting guerrilla warfare while wandering the world. Likewise, we are currently engaged in this game without a home. In this foundation, which is like a platform representing the global representative… Just as God penetrated the satanic world and expanded it, we must do the same. God cannot break this world and recreate it. Therefore, we must occupy this place and expand the foundation. This game, which is currently being trained and practiced globally, is the activity of our mobilization team. 
From now on, what emerges will be our property. From now on, the new members will become our people. Therefore, we must develop this place by any means necessary and desperately seize from the satanic world. We must seek it out. 
However, now that Christianity has established a democratic world, it has created a foundation where faith freedom, assembly freedom, and all basic rights are permitted, making it impossible to treat us as enemies. Therefore, if we can move just one nation, America, quickly, the world will turn around within three years. At most, it will take seven years. 
So, why did God create the democratic world? It was established as a system to facilitate the replacement. All replacements can be made easily… Replacement is necessary. If we unite globally, we can replace the presidential system. Everything can be replaced. When we talk about democracy, ideologically, many think of it as liberalism, but it is not. From the perspective of God's providence, you must understand that it is a means to facilitate the replacement between heavenly people and the satanic world.
So what is the secret to being able to do that? It’s simple. If you go out for 10 years, 14 years, or 20 years, you can become any head of an institution. If you decide to live for the 7-year course, 14-year course, or 21-year course, you will become a leader in any company you enter. Therefore, once you hold onto something, you must invest more than 7 years of dedication. This is the principle. So you need to know that you have a 7-year course. If you cannot achieve it within 7 years, then it will take 21 years (3×7=21). This is the same principle as when Jacob sought his family. From this perspective, even though we are few in number now, when we unite and become one with the teacher, God will develop us entirely.

Why is that? Principally, why is that? It is because we have entered the realm of completion, so Satan cannot accuse us, and God can act. For God to act, we must be completely one with Him. Therefore, if you become completely one with the teacher, this movement can make significant progress. This is principled. It is principled.

The significance of the collapse of the communist world and the events of 1978 in America
So during this conference, there are people receiving teachings from the spirit world about what the teacher is doing. The spirits teaching are of the prophetic type. They bring titles from the prophets who taught during the Old Testament, just as they did in the New Testament. Do you know how such people appear? They are those from the New Testament era. You need to understand that they appear to indemnify the historical lineage. When a free environment is established, the spirit world cooperates, so you do not need to evangelize. We are supposed to dominate the spirit world, not the other way around. It is God's will to have the spirit world handle all worldly affairs.

From this perspective, all the people in the spirit world are on the teacher's side. They all want to support the teacher. And the members of the Unification Church are also on the teacher's side. However, the current world, the external world, is not on that side. (Pointing to what he wrote) What is this in between? It is that there is no spirit world; the stage only has the realm of substance, and what has emerged from this is the materialistic view centered on substance. The period during which Satan was expelled from the spirit world and established a foundation on substance was 40 years; originally, it was 60 years. This period, from 1917 to 1977, was the 60 years granted to Satan.

Now, when that time comes, the world of Satan will begin to collapse in the opposite direction. It started to collapse 21 years ago, 20 years ago. The communist world began to have disputes centered around this period from 1957. The communists are all like this. All the communist worlds that had disputes starting from 1957 will fight for 21 years and then collapse. They must collapse.

This goes until 1977 and 1978, and if we do not establish a foundation by then, it will be extended again. Then it will be a big problem. Why will it be a big problem? Because we will completely lose the foundation of Christianity worldwide. That’s a big problem.

In America, those who are still patriotic or concerned about Christianity are all people over 40. They are mostly in their 50s. They are people who are 20 years apart from those who are close to 60. So if these people move, they can move all of America. However, if this is prolonged, the current streaking trends will become the center, and we will lose the opportunity.

Because the principle is like this, when it does not happen, God cannot act, and the side of Satan will be at the forefront, causing activities that cannot be avoided. This is the principle. If we cannot take responsibility, we will stumble into Satan's trap. This is not something the teacher is just thinking and saying. History is unfolding like this.

Therefore, what is Satan? Those who are playing Satan's games, the ones at the forefront of the Satanic world, are the younger generation. They are the ones who are running around naked. This kind of play is happening. Just like in the Garden of Eden, they acted naked in the Garden of Eden, so they are playing that way. Heaven is using young people…. If we continue to follow God's principles steadily, the world of Satan will keep changing.

The 3rd 7-year course that we must walk on the foundation of victory
However, because we do not change, the world of Satan keeps collapsing, and we, on the contrary, keep developing. As a result, they will be absorbed and transition to a new world. The more we go, the more hope we have, the more confidence we gain, and history becomes clear to us, but they, the more they go, the less they understand the world, and they become more and more frustrated. They are getting further away.

From this perspective, what time is it now? It is the last year of the global 3-year course centered on the teacher. Based on the spiritual foundation, this time is that time. Now, on the foundation that the teacher has fought and won, there remains the 3rd 7-year course that you must walk. You have a foundation to freely act for 7 years centered on this America.

By establishing America as a representative of one world before the will of heaven, you can become citizens of God's nation and children of God by fulfilling the condition of having restored this one nation that is in a fallen position. You must understand that this is the global 3rd 7-year course established to grant you such privileges. You must become the founding warriors of the heavenly nation. Do you understand? “Yes.” You must know that the world revolves around these principles.

So, how do you feel after hearing the teacher's words? Will it happen or not? “It will happen.” Then you understand now. Now I must teach you the secret of victory. (Applause)

Traditions to leave for descendants and the secret to overcoming Satan
Until now, there have been no parents in this universe. Parents have been evil parents, using and ruining their children, all of them. As a result, what was broken? Perfect siblings were broken apart. Then, perfect husbands and wives were broken apart. After that, perfect parents were broken apart. So, they did not have good children. In the end, they lost the family. That family represents the universe. It represented the world, the heavenly nation, and the entire family.

God is trying to find that central point. Human history is also seeking that. Today’s humanity, the people living now, must connect to that center. In other words, the common purpose desired by God and humans is this one thing, and the only way for the past, present, and future to be connected is through this.

So who must do that? What Adam and Eve were supposed to do must now be done by the True Parents. Therefore, what you must have is the brotherhood that Satan does not have, the brotherhood that does not exist in the evil world. You must be like that. That is until your 20s, until you get married. You must leave such a tradition.

You must leave a tradition that says you must live like this in front of your sons and daughters. The struggles you endure in various countries are for the sake of leaving a tradition for your descendants, so that you can educate your children by saying, “We worked hard in such difficult circumstances,” and you must understand that this is a wonderful, once-in-a-lifetime period to gather traditional materials to leave as a will. Therefore, tradition is the issue. This cannot be changed. It is an eternal tradition, an eternal tradition.

We are people who transcend the world, so whites and blacks must become one brotherhood. We must become better brothers than our black brothers. What does that mean? It means we are entering the brotherhood of unfallen humanity, the brotherhood of Adam and Eve. Do you understand? “Yes.”

Then what is the fundamental ideology for establishing such a tradition? It is to serve. You must serve. Then from here, your sons and daughters can grow up in an environment without hardship and become descendants with a direct connection to heaven, possessing a realm of achievement that surpasses the world of Satan. After that, such brothers will marry. For us, marriage is transnational. We can marry a black person, a white person, or an Asian person; we have entered this realm.

Such a tradition must be established from now on. It is not established yet. We must create one from now on. Because of this, you must have that material to lead your descendants and the world. However, if the two do not become one, they must not give birth to evil sons and daughters. To give birth to good sons and daughters, the couple must be completely united. Without unity, good sons and daughters cannot be born. Therefore, they must be completely one centered on God's will.

What is the fall? It is being united centered on Satan. So, conversely, if we are united centered on God absolutely…. If we become one centered on the evil Satan, we will give birth to evil children, but since we are united centered on God, we will give birth to good children. However, that does not mean that the children you give birth to will have three eyes and six hands. (Laughter) It means they will be the same.

What is different is that they will not be like Adam and Eve, who were indecisive. There will never be betrayal against God. If we say, “This is it,” centered on God, we will stick to “this” until the end. From the time of birth until death, it will be like that. That is the difference. Therefore, if a person is unchanging, that person is undoubtedly a person of the heavenly nation.

Only on the day when such a family is established can we serve the archangel, which is the principle of heaven and earth, so even if we go to the world of Satan, Satan will naturally submit. This is the law of heaven. If we do not do so, we will receive a direct hit from God. We will be eternally expelled. If I go and sit among Satan, if they do not submit, I will have to pack my things and leave; that is the principle. That is the principle. Therefore, a person who says, “I will become such a person, day or night, I will become such a person,” cannot be opposed by Satan. They will cooperate.

You must be those who can inherit even nations
Now, have you learned the secret to overcoming Satan? “Yes.” Now, even while eating, you should think, “Ah, I am a true son of God, a true daughter of God! I live beautifully like this, and even though I live in the world of Satan, I become a son or daughter whom Satan cannot accuse, becoming a wonderful husband and wife whom Satan cannot accuse, and becoming completely one with God to give birth to good sons and daughters!” That is how it should be. If you give birth to good sons and daughters, a good lineage and a good world will automatically be established. If you become such a family, you will go directly to heaven. Isn’t that what heaven should be?

However, we must not be without a nation while having a family. We must create a family based on a nation. To prevent Satan from invading, the world is invading centered on the nation, but if we establish a nation that Satan cannot invade, this world will become God’s nation. Now, do you understand? “Yes.”

Until now, humanity did not know how humans would become. They did not know how they would become. They did not know history. They did not know where the present is becoming what. They did not know what the future would hold.

Why is that? Because they did not have true parents, true ancestors. However, by having True Parents, we can say, “Ah, I have understood history. I have understood the history between God and me.” We have also understood the present. We have understood the future. Not only that, but we can inherit such a tradition. I can now have a tradition that can overcome history and the future.

From whom? Why? Because I met True Parents. I follow what True Parents teach, I desire what they desire, and I inherit this. That is what it means to receive the lineage.

Now, men should think, “Ah, I must be like the teacher.” Women should think, “Ah, I must be like the mother.” They do not doubt God even if they die. They do not think of denying the principles centered on themselves or trying to stand out. They go according to the principles. They must be better than Adam and Eve.

By doing so, you must inherit your family. You must become qualified to inherit the traditions left by your parents, inherit the family, and that family must inherit the lineage. Then your lineage must inherit the nation, your nation must inherit the world, and your world must inherit God. You must understand that without establishing a sacrificial foundation in these larger areas, you cannot connect the basis for inheritance and exchange.

Even if you know everything, you can pass on all traditions to you right now, but what can you inherit? You can only inherit a family. You can only inherit a lineage. You can inherit this kind of foundation. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” If there had been no fall, to what extent? To the nation, to the world, everything would be inherited. You inherit everything. Just by establishing that family, everything will become yours, but it is not like that now. That is why the teacher’s ultimate purpose must be how quickly to pass on the nation’s traditions to you before he dies. (The recording briefly stops)

Sovereignty must be connected like this. All order is established this way. Life must be lived this way. Happiness is like this. Therefore, we cannot be without a nation. We cannot be without a nation. However, we do not have a nation.

So, since we have gathered here in this free land of America, we must put in all our sincerity. However, America is made up of 50 states. I thought there would be at least 70 states, but 50 states seem a bit small. If there were about 40 states, it would be just right in terms of the principle…. (Laughter) What is truly grateful is that each state has different laws. The central government can also boycott; they all can. So this is like one nation. Therefore, when we turn just three states, America will turn. If we just set up seven states, America will be completely caught.

Imagine if there are 500 people like you in one state. We can handle the Senate elections and the formation of Congress. (Laughter) There is no faster way to rise than this path of ours.

Think about how much influence the teacher has had in America in just 1 year and 7 months and how famous he has become. If we take what has been proclaimed here and bring it back to Korea to hold an exhibition in a large auditorium, the Korean people will react like this. (Making a face) (Laughter, applause) If it rises like this in America, Korea will completely submit. Then, based on this established America, we will connect with about 70 countries worldwide.
If you put it in place, then at that time, the United States can be completely abandoned. 
Imagine if we mobilize about 7,000 people and go to a country, and just run in 7 cities in each state. What would happen? Just with those 7 cities, it would be a huge impact. If we then use the media to say, "Do well, do well," and if we receive aid, it will turn around immediately. Therefore, I believe that the world uniting is not far off.

The teacher is not a dreamer but a theorist. And not only does he leave the theory as it is, but he also puts it into practice. Moreover, he does not practice it poorly compared to others. He practices it better than others, so the world is destined to unite. This is theoretical. Thus, the Korean government is learning a lot from the operations I am conducting. The United States is also learning a lot from my methods, all of them. When we do various things like this, everyone automatically imitates me, and then naturally, they come under my command and into our intentions. (Laughter. Applause) This movement is a global event and a historical event that we must recognize.

You might think, "No matter how much we do, what has changed from yesterday to today, from last year to now? The teacher says that the will will be fulfilled, but I don't quite understand that." You don't have to worry about that. However, you must recognize that even though you are alone, you are not the same. The reason is that you are becoming specialized in your work. You become so skilled that just by looking at someone, you can tell whether that person will campaign for you or not, whether they will listen to you or not. You must understand that becoming an expert is essential.

It's just like the difference between someone graduating from middle school and someone receiving a university degree; it's the same. What has changed? The internal area of expertise has changed. Your area of expertise has expanded. You must recognize that you are "eating the invisible historical wealth!"

Three requirements to become a responsible leader
To succeed, a person must know how to speak, then know how to engage in diplomacy, and finally, know how to make money. You must be able to do all three. To be a complete leader, you cannot just excel in one of these areas. Being good at speaking alone is not enough, and being good at socializing is not enough either. If you lack any of these, you cannot become a leader. All three must be present. If even one is missing, you cannot be a complete leader.

The teacher has been someone who has set goals and trained for this since childhood. He can speak anywhere, at any time. He can talk about the spiritual world and the future. He can speak even without preparation. He has had a lot of experience.

When I look around, there are all kinds of types. If I see someone who was once my friend and had some relationship with me, that becomes the title. When it comes to someone who has experienced sad events, if I weave the topic around their feelings and stories from that time, I can bring tears and amazement, and through the subject, the other person is automatically influenced. It's the same.

When you go to campaign and ask for money, if you get slapped and fall down with a nosebleed, that becomes a valuable historical material. It becomes a resource that can touch millions of people. Think about how such a situation can be a treasure that can move millions.

When you place millions in such a position and speak while realizing such scenes, all your strength comes out. Imagine pouring out the expression and emotions of joy when the times of frustration turn into the opposite. Create such environments every day, gathering materials and packing them away.

Since communication is not smooth, if you express your feelings with gestures and then cry out of frustration, how wonderful would that scene be? In that moment, the world and the spirits of the spiritual world bow their heads. It becomes a great opportunity for my supporting troops to emerge.

By sharing such stories, how much fire will it ignite in the hearts of the youth in the future! When it comes time to save not only your own country but also other countries, it becomes a source to mobilize all the youth of each country and send them out into the world. Therefore, persecution is not bad, suffering is not bad, and the path of death is not bad. You must think of it as a solemn place to inherit the materials that can move history. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

The teacher is the same. The teacher has trained in speaking because he knows he must be able to speak. He also knows he must engage in diplomacy. Therefore, I have met all the people I need in the United States. They must have thought it was strange that Reverend Moon comes to the Senate every day with a bundle. (Laughter) Because I had already established relationships at that time, due to the Watergate incident, they completely sided with me. They all advertised, "Ah, Reverend Moon is passionate, old, but a good person, a genius." So I became quite well-known.

In the future, even without an appointment, if I just walk into a senator's office and there is a senator, they will drop everything and say, "Welcome." That day is not far off. (Applause) Because I have met all of them, when you go on a tour, all the Senate experts will be there... In places like New York, they will give you a room, which is scarier than a bomb. "Boom!" Why is Reverend Moon able to gather such significant people, the top officials of the nation? The celebration is about bringing out your own banner... All at once, even the CIA, FBI, and all sorts of people will be completely caught up in it. Therefore, what proclamation? "Ah, a congratulatory message from a senator, and the president knows about it, what's going on?" With one word, all problems are resolved.

Last night, I met someone from this city who said that being in the presence of the esteemed Reverend Moon made their heart tremble, and their heart was racing. (Laughter)

In the future, there will come a time when one word can change all ambassadors. April 29, 1974 (Monday), Headquarters Church.
* This message is also published in Message No. 162 (July 10, 1974).
Our Unification Church and Me
I could have had the mindset to say that I am also a Unificationist, but now, I 
believe the time has come for our Unification Church to institutionalize. There 
is a system for the headquarters, a system for the provinces, and a system for 
the districts. The time has passed when we could act without acknowledging 
such systems.
This is because, to move the entire world, it cannot be done with just the 
relationship between you and me. There must be a vertical relationship, and 
without following the principles of hierarchy, order, and the relationships of 
front and back, left and right, it is impossible to dominate the world.
Therefore, I hope you will first recognize that such training is necessary in 
our Unification Church today. You may feel disappointed if guests are sent away, 
but please understand it that way. Originally, I intended to speak centered 
around the church leaders and the church heads. Since you are here, one thing I 
want to say in front of you is “Our Unification Church and Me.” I will speak 
with this title.
Today, I am a representative of the nation and the world within the Unification 
Church.
Our Unification Church has now truly become a global religion. You in Korea, 
centered on the Unification Church in Korea, refer to the Unification Church 
spread throughout the world as “our Unification Church.” In Japan, the members 
there refer to it as “our Unification Church” centered around Japan. The members 
in America also refer to the church in America as “our Unification Church.” 
Currently, when we say “our,” it is centered around the meaning of “our,” and 
everyone should understand this.
Now, when we think of “Our Unification Church and Me,” we often forget the 
concept of “me” within that “our.” Although we say “our Unification Church,” 
we often forget that “me” represents the whole. It is easy to forget that “me” 
is the representative of the whole. Because Unification Church members refer to 
each other as family, they see it as “whether one came first or later, we are all 
the same family. We are all the same!” This way of thinking has been a problem 
up until now.
As the number of family members grows and the number of church members increases, 
we must recognize that the “our” represents more and more the whole. Our 
Unification Church is not centered on the East. Within the Unification Church of 
the East, there are nations, and the entire world is included. Therefore, today, 
the “me” must not only be centered on the East but must also be a “me” that can 
transcend the nation and encompass the world.
When evangelizing, we must not think, “It must be me.” We should not evangelize 
only for a specific region or locality, but rather with the mindset of representing 
the entire world. When we evangelize someone, we should think, “This person is 
someone I evangelized. Because of my relationship with them, they are my 
spiritual child.” Instead, we must recognize that “I am in a vertical relationship 
with them as a child representing the world.”
Therefore, while we enter the society of the Unification Church, we must realize 
that we are not limited to that society alone. If things go wrong, the repercussions 
will reach the nation or even the world, and we must recognize that we are in an 
era that is different from the past. Because when Japanese members act for the 
sake of America, if something goes wrong there, even though they are members of 
the Unification Church in Japan, they will be held accountable from a position 
representing the world.
Thus, the relationship between our Unification Church and me is not limited to 
“our Unification Church and me” within Korea. We must recognize that this is 
shifting to an era where we can represent the nation and the world. Therefore, 
the activities you are engaged in should not stop here but should be expanded to 
connect with global activities. You must understand that we have entered an era 
where the results achieved here today should not remain as results related only to 
yourself but should remain as results connected to the world.
In that sense, every word you say and every action you take should not leave 
limited results. If you are going to a training session in your locality, you must 
understand that it is not just for that training but that you are moving with the 
historical destiny of the world on your shoulders.
From this perspective, in the midst of the restoration of the cosmos, you must 
always criticize your position from such a standpoint and always be aware that 
you are representing that position. You must understand that one person can ruin 
the world and one person can bring shame to the world; this era is approaching us.
Therefore, you should not think, “If I want to go to the headquarters, I will go 
as I please. Who can stop me when I go on my own feet?” You must understand this.
It is time to think about the system and to build an organization.
What I have feared the most until now is that when people working in the 
localities come to the headquarters, I have often met them directly. Then, when 
the association president sits in the same place as me, the cultural department head 
can come in, and anyone can come in with that mindset. However, you must understand 
that this is an extremely difficult issue.
It is a very important issue, and even when discussing secret matters that no one 
should know, matters of national importance, grandmothers come in carrying 
baskets of rice and sit down, dozing off. (Laughter) Some young ladies come in and 
just greet… While greetings are appreciated, who is asking for greetings? 
Greetings are appreciated, but they should consider what the current situation is 
and how the environment is. They just come in without thinking… It’s a real 
problem. I can’t just tell them to leave as soon as they come in. (Laughter) 
They come in earnestly and greet me earnestly, but if I say something, they might 
think, “Oh, the Teacher doesn’t recognize me! Things have changed. When I was in 
Korea, it was still good, but after going to America, he has become just like an 
American!” (Laughter) Because of this tendency, even if I wink at them, they don’t 
understand. (Laughter) Yet, I can’t just kick them out… Such incidents are 
common.
Now, looking at this, you all need to start thinking about the system. The 
issue of what corruption is or where confusion arises is also related to where 
these things occur. Confusion arises when the relationships of front and back, 
left and right become entangled. We must understand that this is where 
deviation occurs.
What is corruption? You must understand that it originates from the fact that 
the person who should be in front has fallen behind. Corruption is determined 
based on principles, and the positions of all principled beings are established, 
and the original ideal type is fulfilled. If we deny the principles and say that 
everyone should go together at once, and moreover, if we say that I will eat 
everything delicious, that should not be the case. Of course, we all know the 
circumstances, but we should not excuse them.
Therefore, it is now time for you to think about the system and to establish 
an organization. I hope you first recognize this. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
What a good response! Unification Church members are good at responding. But 
when I say directly, “Do it this way!” they become sullen.
Corruption began with emphasizing “me” over “us.”
When we look at the perspective of “Our Unification Church and Me,” in order for 
our Unification Church to go global, you must act in a way that can represent the 
world. Even when greeting, you must greet in a way that can represent the world, 
and you must become the “me” that heaven desires. When you speak, you must speak 
in a manner that can respectfully represent the world. This is the “me” that heaven 
desires. All matters, although limited to the relationship between the individual 
and the church, have passed the era where they can be resolved only within that 
limit; we have entered a time when we must consider the whole and resolve 
accordingly. Please understand this. Do you understand? “Yes.”
From now on, when you have a name like Kim Anyoung or Kim Jayu, you must 
clearly see whether the “Kim” is “Kim” or “Jeon.” If it says Jeon Jayu but Kim 
Jayu comes up, that would be a big problem. You must confirm that it is definitely 
my name, Kim Jayu, Jeon Jayu, and it must be definitely Kim Jayu.
From now on, we must filter such things, and we cannot avoid holding such 
meetings. The Teacher does not have that much time. If we cannot finish today’s 
meeting, we will have to continue until tomorrow… There are many special issues 
that need to be addressed. If there are issues I can teach you, I can do it through 
the church heads who guide you. So, it is difficult to do it this way. Do you 
understand? Do you comprehend? “Yes.”
You might think, “I thought the Teacher would share good stories, but instead, he 
has quietly laid everything out so we can’t move at all.” You might feel 
disappointed, but you should not feel that way. Feeling disappointed is to be 
self-centered, but when viewed from the perspective of the entire world, I am 
speaking words that are natural.
Therefore, when you think about the issue of “Our Unification Church and Me,” 
everything changes. When people think about whether I am close or we are close, 
which is closer? “I am closer.” I am closer. “We are far apart.” This way of 
thinking has been the thought process in this fallen world until now. Which is 
more precious? When asked whether we are precious or I am precious, I am precious. 
When asked what should be better, it should be that I am better than our 
Unification Church. All these issues arise from there.

Three Essential Requirements for a Leader
What is the philosophy that the teacher has held until now? A leader has three major issues, and these are considered important, life-giving elements. When we talk about the important requirements for a leader, there are three major principles. First, what is it? A leader must be able to persuade the group under their command. They must be able to speak with eloquence that can move people. The first requirement is that they must know how to speak. They must be able to gather the public, inspire them, and present a goal that they can comply with. If someone cannot speak in this way, they cannot be a leader. To be someone who can speak, it should not be common knowledge. It must be knowledge that others do not know, and at the same time, it must be the truth. When the unknown truth becomes a fact, everyone will comply with it. To reach that position, what is needed? Skill is the issue. You must possess skill.

Next, what is it? You must know how to conduct diplomacy. The Unification Church has come this far because the teacher has orchestrated everything behind the scenes. During the era of Chairman Yoo and Chairman Kim, whenever a special incident occurred, I directed everything. "Today, a detective will come here, so you need to prepare." At that time, we would extend our antennas. Do you understand? Then, "If you say this, do it this way. I will pray for you. Then by the afternoon, it will turn out like this." This is the kind of struggle we have gone through. You must know how to conduct diplomacy by putting people forward rather than stepping in directly. You must also know how to conduct diplomacy yourself. You need to have the capability to absorb and utilize the foundation that others have laid. In other words, you must be skilled in diplomacy. This is the second major principle that a leader must possess.

Then, what is the third? You must know how to manage economic power. Economic power. Today, even a nation is facing issues, right? There must be a national policy, a national policy. There must be a slogan that can guide and persuade the national citizens. Then, it must become a public discourse that they can welcome and be inspired by. After that, it requires economic power that can flourish the foundation and unite it as one. This is always necessary. These are the three essential elements in any issue. Therefore, for us individuals to become leaders, we must know how to utilize economic power as the third principle.

If you cannot solve money issues and apply money to the necessary purposes, you cannot become a leader. No matter how well you utilize money and how good you are at diplomacy, if you cannot speak, you are fundamentally lacking. No matter how good you are at diplomacy and speaking, if you cannot utilize economic power, you are lacking. The important principles of being a complete leader are these three principles. The teacher has adopted these three principles as a philosophy of life.

April 30, 1974, Instructions at the National Leaders' Meeting in Korea  
1. Current Issues  
1) The Essential Attitude of a Faithful Believer  
a. Personal Independence and Defense  
You must achieve personal independence. Then you must know how to defend yourself. What was the fall in Eden? It was the failure to achieve personal independence. They fell because they did not know how to defend themselves. Therefore, you must become someone who knows how to achieve personal independence and defense. This is the first issue of the essential attitude of a faithful believer. Do you understand?  
b. Family Independence and Defense  
In a family, you must be able to achieve independence centered around the family. Do not rely on anyone. You must know how to achieve independence and defend yourself in the faith line centered around your wife or children.  
c. Church Independence and Defense  
You, as church leaders, must think about how to make the church independent and how to defend it.  
d. Cooperation for Overall Independence and Defense  
What this means is that, whether it is nationwide or centered around the association, the entire content you are responsible for must be able to achieve independence. Only then can we promote development in each field; if the independent foundation in one field collapses, it will be like a hole that lets water flow out. Therefore, we must cooperate for overall independence and defense. If something is better on one side, it should be passed over, and if something cannot be done on one side, it should be received from the other side. We must establish a system of independence and defense that can be utilized mutually and cooperate on average.  
2) The Division of Good and Evil  
Today, we cannot overlook this issue. The division of good and evil, how do we divide good and evil?  
a. Centered on Principle and Tradition  
You must understand that God divides based on principle and tradition. Do you understand? Centered on principle, the principle of creation, and centered on the tradition that God must establish, we must understand that division occurs.  
b. The Point of Unity between Subject and Object

Until now, Satan has been opposing us, and because of the Communist Party, the victory alliance has been able to develop, right? “Yes.” (Laughter)
In that sense, it’s good either way. If Satan opposes, that also benefits my side, and if there is no opposition, that also benefits my side, so it’s good either way. Because I think of such principles, I hope that the tedious battles that God has fought through the historical age will definitely lead to such results. The one who will decide this may be the Unification Church’s Moon Sun-myung. Do you understand? “Yes.”
How do you feel when you hear such words? You’ve never heard them before, right? “Yes.” If you don’t know that, you can’t solve the problem. You need to know something to use it. To use it, you need to know the legal provisions, and based on these provisions, this happens, and based on these provisions, that happens, and you need something that can prove that this contract is certain and that the state and society can represent it. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” Now, it’s not just about writing, but the teacher is doing this work. That’s why the teacher is three years ahead of you.
Until now, I have scattered a lot of eagle food in the fields, but now I need to go harvest. New things will unfold. I will handle everything, and that is the principle. Do you understand? “Yes.”
All of this is possible because we have reached such a day as the victory ceremony. The teacher has suffered for 20 years…. The teacher has suffered, right? “Yes.” Alone, alone. There are no friends. Parents don’t know. I am all alone.
Standing in the position of the parents after the fall of Adam, I have taken on the responsibilities that the parents should bear and have come out alone. Since I have come this far, now I will take a break. I will put my children forward, and for three years, let’s make the world shine. We are going up. The established church is going down. Just wait and see. We are going up. That’s how you should understand it. Huh? “Yes.” Those who understood, raise your hands. Then don’t forget it. Huh? “Yes.” You tend to forget well, always. (Laughter) Don’t listen to other words. There is no one like the teacher. Have you ever felt so grateful that tears flowed and you laughed until your teeth fell out?
Those who assert themselves should pack their bags. 
Those who complain centered around themselves should pack their bags and leave! (Due to poor recording quality, some parts could not be recorded) Until now, the teacher has known everything but pretended not to know. Mr. Ok Se-hyun, how many fights have you had? Let’s see who loves this path. If you know, there’s a reason you can’t die. If you dislike this, pack your bags and go live. Go outside the fence. The main culprit is still remaining. Do you understand? Do you old ladies understand? How much have you done for the teacher and for heaven?

7)
Me and the Present
<Prayer> Father, we welcome May with this first new Sabbath morning. As the children gather before You to welcome this new day and this new month, may they bow before You with new hearts and new intentions; have mercy on them and love them.

Father, among the children gathered here, representing the world among Your children scattered across the globe, we have a responsibility to present something to You, so please remember us at this time. We dedicate everything before Your will, and we earnestly hope and wish to be children who can absolutely comply with Your desired will and offer ourselves before You.

In every place gathered in Your name on this day, among the many groups following Your will, may Your eternal protection be with them, and may they be able to approach a holy life that can affirm a day of victory.

Father, bless this morning. I earnestly ask and wish that this morning becomes a necessary day in the world of desires You wish for. May everything be fulfilled as You intended. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
May 5, 1974 (Sunday) early morning, Headquarters Church.
* This message was also published in the June 1974 issue of <Unification World>.

<Words> We, humans living on this earth today, know that we look toward the future through the point of today. From that perspective, we understand that there are individuals who remain in such a position, as well as families, tribes, nations, and the world beyond families.

Humans Who Have Lost Their Original World
The present situation we find ourselves in today is established from the position inherited from the past. Today exists because yesterday was there, and tomorrow exists because today is here. From this perspective, we can see that history is necessarily formed through the past, present, and future. We come to understand that everything is determined centered on the present, this point of today.

When we consider the will of God and the present nation, we realize that there has not been a place in the historical course where God's will could be fulfilled today. Since the day humanity fell, the original will that God intended has not yet been realized. In other words, the command “Do not eat from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil” has never been fulfilled without eating from it.

The world of the original will is a place where goodness exists, a place where God's eternal and unchanging love must be present. If we had started from such a standpoint, a true brotherly tradition would have been established. The true brotherly tradition—this brother who has lived in God's love would be the brother whom God is most pleased with—would have remained on this planet.

Furthermore, there would have been a tradition of a couple who could receive God's love, and beyond that, a tradition of true parents. There would have been a tradition of innocent, good children. Thus, centered on a family where God's will has been realized, a tradition would have surely been established.

This is because God's love is present, and at the same time, God's life is present, and God is eternally with them, so evil cannot be established there. The accusation rights of Satan could not exist. Only God could govern, and only God could discern good and evil; if evil existed, that evil would have surely been corrected by God's direct governance.

If such a world had come to be, it would have been the world where God's original will was fulfilled, a world where God's ideals could dwell.

However, humanity's ancestors lost such a position due to the fall. They fell. Where did they fall from? They fell from the world of this will. It is not that they fell from some sky; they deviated from the position of God's original will. After the fall, when humanity was expelled from the Garden of Eden, they were expelled from the position where the will could be fulfilled, based on the place where the will had been realized.

When we think centered on the will, we realize that the position we are in today is not a place where the will has been fulfilled but a fallen world. Currently, we live as individuals, as families, or as South Korea, or as the world in this fallen world. When viewed this way, the position we are living in now has no relation to the world of the will.

Therefore, we must innovate anew here, shake off all these environments, and return anew. That path is the path of faith. The position we are currently in cannot be simply tolerated. We must revolutionize here and eliminate this position. We must understand that going against this path of fate is the path of faith.

For us today, the past is not a past inherited from God's will but a past connected with Satan, so we must settle that past. No matter how good the past was, we must recognize that it is a past that should not be connected with today’s self. We must clearly understand that the past we have lived for decades cannot leave anything that can help our faith journey or influence it in any way.

Eliminate the habitual tendencies acquired within the realm of the fall
For humans, habitual tendencies are terrifying. If you are South Korean, you like kimchi and pickled radish. Once this habit is established, when sitting at the table, you inevitably think of the habitual kimchi and gochujang. No matter how good something is, you don’t accept it positively; rather, you judge its taste based on the old habitual tendencies.

From this perspective, we come to realize how terrifying the habitual tendencies of humans living in the fallen world today are. For instance, if a person from the North comes down to the South, they are of the same ethnicity and share similar lifestyles, but because they stand in different social environments or directions, their habits or ideas cannot be easily canceled.

I have felt this deeply; after being in the South and then going to the North for several years, it took me at least three years to resolve all the feelings from the North after returning to the South. I have experienced that it takes more than three years. From this perspective, we must recognize how much our habitual tendencies hinder our faith life and how much faith is distorted due to these tendencies.

In this light, we must understand that the current “me” living today is not a position that can be recognized by God in terms of faith. Therefore, we must completely eliminate the habitual tendencies of the past acquired within the realm of the fall. This includes not only the life I have lived but also friends, family, or society related to me; wherever we are, we must recognize that the environment does not align with the content that can contribute to the fulfillment of the will that heaven desires in the world of faith.

We must always adjust our lives today based on God as the standard
When we decide what is good and bad, it is often the case that the majority decides based on themselves. “Oh! That’s good!” “Oh! That’s bad.” When making such judgments, whose standard is it? It is not the standard that God desires but the standard that I desire. It is a statement made from the position I find myself in, influenced by my past life habits.

Those who have lived well tend to judge based on the standards of their good habits, while those who have lived poorly tend to judge based on their poor circumstances. Therefore, we must recognize that there are vast differences.

God’s will is unchangeable. No matter how many people there are, there is only one path toward the will. Because God is absolute, the will is one, and the path toward that will cannot be two. It cannot be a matter of coming and going as one pleases. There is only one path. We must think that there can only be a straight line. When viewed this way, the judgments we have made about what is good and bad until now do not stand on a standard that represents the whole but are based solely on our own life habits.

Thus, what is the most precious thing in carrying out a life of faith? It is how to forget the past and seek something new. This is the most critical issue. If we cannot live such a life, we must return from the world of evil. The evil world flows in this way, and we cannot return to the world of God's original will while keeping pace with this flow. Therefore, we must deny the current position flowing and escape from here.

To overcome this environment and establish a breakthrough in a new aspect, we must find a path that does not follow the same direction every day; this is the path of faith that leads to the world God desires. Therefore, in order to walk the path of faith, we must recognize that our strength is insufficient and that we lack any habitual or lifestyle standards centered on God, which makes it easy for us to change. Thus, we must always adjust our lives today based on God as the standard.

No matter how good the past may be, we must recognize that we cannot connect that past with the present life of the will. That past is not aligned with the discerned will of God but is ultimately a past of the world of Satan. Even if we went out for the sake of the will, the past we left behind in the process of fighting and discerning does not align with the will.

From this perspective, a person must inherit the past, but the question is where to find that past. Where should the past be set as a standard? The past must be right; if it is not right, we cannot find the right path in the present. Therefore, the question is what we set as the basis for that past. Today, many religions face this issue; if they do not make efforts to inherit the intentions of their founders, whether they are prophets or religious leaders, they cannot inherit the standards of the religion established within God's will during that era.

By inheriting such a past, we can delineate the direction of a new religion in pioneering a realistic foundation that can be guaranteed by that past. If we cannot inherit such a past, we will not have a reality that aligns with the will of God or the will of any religion. It is only from the position where the past and present are united that we can find a path to the new future; we cannot think that there can be a future standing in a position where the past and present are not aligned.

We must go beyond the standards of past failures and establish a victorious foundation
From this perspective, when we look at Christianity today, which religion is centered on whom? It is centered on Jesus. In the New Testament era, we must start centered on Jesus. The footprints of the life Jesus lived for 33 years do not end with His own life; rather, they become a foundation for all Christians today to seek the world of the future. Only through efforts to establish today’s self, which can inherit the reality of life on that foundation, can we walk the path of God's will. If we cannot do this, the current position cannot align with God's will, and we must recognize that we can easily become someone who betrays God's will because Satan can take that foundation as its own. 

Therefore, today, we believers must certainly look at the Bible.
의 땅에서 벗어나 본연의 세계로 돌아가려면 완전한 부정과 완전한 분별이 필요합니다. 

하나님은 우리에게 사탄을 부정하고, 사탄의 세계에서 벗어나 본연의 세계로 돌아가라고 요구하십니다. 이는 단순히 사탄을 이기는 것이 아니라, 사탄의 모든 영향을 완전히 제거하고, 하나님이 주관하시는 세계로 나아가야 한다는 것을 의미합니다. 타락하지 않은 본연의 자리에는 사탄이 없었고, 오직 하나님만이 계셨습니다. 

그러므로 우리는 사탄을 부정하고, 그 환경을 극복해야 합니다. 예수님은 “모든 것을 다 버리고 나를 따르라”고 말씀하셨습니다. 이는 완전한 부정과 분별을 요구하는 것입니다. 우리는 사탄의 세계에서 벗어나 새로운 길을 찾아야 하며, 그 길은 고독하고 힘든 길일 수 있습니다. 하지만 그 길을 가야만 하늘나라에 이를 수 있습니다.

오늘날 우리가 사는 대한민국은 사탄권에 포위되어 있습니다. 이 세계에서 하늘나라로 가기 위해서는 가장 불쌍한 자리, 즉 사탄이 가장 싫어하는 자리로 나아가야 합니다. 이 자리에서 우리는 하늘나라의 출발점을 찾을 수 있습니다. 

우리가 살고 있는 대한민국의 역사와 하나님의 뜻은 결코 일치할 수 없습니다. 대한민국의 성인 역사와 하나님의 뜻의 성인 역사는 다릅니다. 이러한 운명 속에서 우리는 본연의 땅으로 돌아가기 위해 완전한 부정과 분별이 필요하다는 것을 깨달아야 합니다.
How can we find the original ideal realm that we have not yet achieved? We must escape from this. We must break through the boundaries. It is our personal boundaries that are blocking us. We can feel that. Generally, it is our families that block us. Who blocks our personal boundaries? Of course, our environment and our habitual inertia do, but more directly, it is the family that is the problem.

For a husband, the wife is the problem, and for parents, the children are the problem. Therefore, the saying that "your family members are your enemies" is valid here. My family members are my enemies. Even though there is a path of destiny that I must take, if I do not go, it leads to death. In breaking through this path of death, who is blocking me? In my heart, it is my body, but even more so, it is the reality that is directly confronting me: the wife in front of the husband, and the husband in front of the wife. The children in front of the parents, and the parents in front of the children.

Then, what is in front of the family? The issue is the tribe. The issue is the kinship. What is the problem in front of the tribe? It is the nation. In front of the nation, the issue is the state. The state establishes national policies centered around itself and carries out politics that suit that nation. Isn't that right? This politics does not align with the will of God. In transcending nationalism, because the state prevents it, countless people who follow this new will of God are sacrificed, and the history of martyrdom cannot be avoided. You must understand this. Expanding on this, in trying to go beyond the nation to the world, there must again be a confrontation.

Do you have a past that you can boast about before heaven?
Now, when you look at this, you must ask yourself whether you truly have a past that you can boast about before heaven. Do you have it? You must understand that without confirming this, you will not even know when the door to hell will come to you.

Today, people who have entered the Unification Church may say, "Entering the Unification Church is worse than the established church..." But it should not be better than the established church. It should be worse. Do you understand what that means? In terms of living, it should be worse. In walking the path of the will, it should be difficult. There are tears here, there is persecution here, and there is suffering here, and just because a terrible environment unfolds does not mean it is a bad church.

The more difficult it is, the more persecution there is in all areas, the more that persecution is not partial but national, the more that organization has something that can be left as a national entity within the will for the future. We can find this from this perspective.

Among you, if you are walking the path of faith and later lose your center and waver, saying, "Ah, I entered the Unification Church for no reason. I spent ten years in the Unification Church and wasted my youth, and now I'm old, recognize me," who told you to enter the Unification Church? What would happen if you were recognized? The more you are recognized, the more you fall into ruin. If you stand in a position that acknowledges it and says, "You did well," it is the same as burying something alive after establishing it. Why? Because if you acknowledge that you are just staying in the realm of Satan, both you and the Unification Church will perish. You must understand this.

Now, think about it. What has changed between me ten years ago and me ten years later? Aren't you worse off than when you first entered? Isn't your spiritual state worse than when you first entered? What happens if you acknowledge that? Can you be recognized for that? Even if you entered ten years ago, that past you had when you entered does not guarantee a past that can be recognized within God's will.

Therefore, you must deny it. If you hold onto negative elements and ask for your present to be positively connected to a standard, then both the act of being positive and the act of being recognized will perish. Today, you are caught in such a situation.

What is the problem with those who have been in the Unification Church for a long time? There are those who want to be treated well in front of newcomers. Such people are extremely foolish. I see it that way. It is a very dangerous attitude.

To want to be treated well in front of newcomers? Have the newcomers inherited the traditions of the Unification Church? Have they been grafted into a historically guaranteed past that God can recognize? No. The newer you are, the less historical guarantee you have. If you want to elevate yourself from there, it is certain that you are deviating from the essence of faith. You cannot evaluate from that position. You must clearly understand this.

That is why the present self is the most frightening. The fact that I am asking for something means that if I do not drink from the breast of Satan, I must take and eat something from the love of God. It is one or the other. The fact that I am living means that I am either walking the path of death in the realm of Satan or walking the path of life.

However, today, the path of life is far from the realm of Satan, so in order to find the path of life to eat, you cannot just sit and eat. There is no other way than to go to the boundary and receive sustenance through some path. However, today, because we humans are in the realm of Satan, it is difficult to receive this sustenance.

Because we are in such a position today, those who walk the path of faith must pray. That is why prayer is necessary. You must breathe. You must breathe on this suffocating earth. That is why Jesus came to this earth and said, "Pray without ceasing." He did not say to read the Bible without ceasing. He said to pray without ceasing. It is not easy to break through and overcome the realities of the environment. You must understand this clearly.

The representative standards of faith that historical figures walked
How much have you changed since entering the Unification Church? If you have not changed, that past cannot be recognized by God. You must understand that the current position of someone who does not have a past that can be recognized by God is already a position where the before and after are intertwined. This is a serious problem.

So how should you go? We must correct the mistakes made in the Old Testament. We must correct the mistakes made in the New Testament. From this perspective, our Unification Church is saying that we must fulfill the covenant of completing the Old and New Testaments. In the Adam family, since Adam and Eve fell, we must correct the fallen tradition. We must deny that period.

In the Unification Church, if a man has fallen due to love, then the woman must be denied. If the woman has fallen, then the man must be denied. It must be denied to the absolute limit. Without doing so, there is no way to find the correct past standard as a newly called woman or man before heaven.

If you have someone you love, you must regard that person as an enemy. You must discover a merciless self that can cut off and remove that love without hesitation; otherwise, you cannot even imagine the original standard that God intended to achieve with me through the heart's connection and the love of Eden. You cannot even think of it. No matter how beautiful a woman or handsome a man comes to entice you, you must set your own standard of complete denial. Shouldn't it be that way? Otherwise, you cannot correct the sinful history formed by the fallen lineage.

Next, looking at Noah's family, he persevered for 120 years. From the day God commanded him, he steadily... As time went on, rather than getting tired, he had the determination to develop more. As he got older, it would be difficult, and in the daily tasks, there was a position where his sincerity could diminish due to habitual work, but it was not a matter of effort; rather, he increased his sincerity as the days went by. He had to be better than yesterday. He must be better. The fact that he built the ark for 120 years on the top of Mount Ararat is astonishing. If you set a goal, all humanity must steadily continue to seek the heavenly kingdom. The number 120 represents the whole. You must live your entire life consistently.

For Abraham, he stood in a position where he had to sacrifice his son with a knife, a position that is unthinkable in human ethics, but he stood in a position to kill his son for the will of heaven. You must understand that.

Moses also, in front of the path, abandoned all the people he loved, and when he was uncertain, he forsook everything to negotiate, while having a heart that loved heaven more than his own people and ascended Mount Sinai. You must have that kind of heart.

He abandoned all the environments. Moses, who drove 600,000 people into the wilderness and went up to the top of Mount Sinai without saying a word for 40 days, what kind of resolute heart did he have? When he saw that the issue of life and death was urgent at this crossroads, the cries of the nation were not the problem; rather, the question was how heaven viewed it. He disregarded that environment and, like Moses, had to walk the path of a resolute man.

These are the representative types and standards that have appeared in history as figures that humanity must follow in their faith journey.

Consider John the Baptist. He spent 30 years in the wilderness eating locusts and wild honey, regardless of whether the wind blew, it rained, or it snowed. That was not the issue; what he desired was solely to meet the Messiah and live with him. Meeting the Messiah was his goal.

No matter how great the hardships of being rained on, suffering, and being despised, when he realized that the value of the Messiah could not be compared to anything, he could treat those hardships as nothing. John the Baptist must have had a dignified perspective. If he had wanted to complain, he could not have spent over 30 years living in the wilderness. Think about how he lived in the wilderness, eating locusts and wild honey and wearing a leather belt. Would he have worn a suit like today or shoes? He must have walked barefoot. Even now, when you go to Israel, people walk barefoot.

Such John the Baptist was a subject of ridicule in his time. When he walked around the neighborhood, even children would say, "Look at that!" How would his parents and relatives feel? Would they have promoted him as "Oh! The prophet sent by God, our beloved John the Baptist!"? How would his parents have reacted? Think about it. It is shameful. What kind of shame would it be for his brothers to see him? Wouldn't it be the greatest shame?

When you look at such figures, they were not those who were revered by the social environment of their time; they were all ridiculed. However, no matter how difficult the environment was, no matter what opposed them, they knew that the coming Messiah transcended the nation and the world, and that he was a being of invaluable worth that could not be exchanged for anything. Therefore, they did not regard that existence as a problem. These are the representative figures who do not regard such things as problems.

Look at Jesus. When Jesus came to this earth, he completely cut off the Judaism that the Israelite nation had institutionalized and formalized. He rebuked them, saying, "You brood of vipers!" Look at how fiercely he confronted them. He said, "You and I cannot sit together." Rather, he said that those who do not believe are closer to him. It cannot be helped. It is incredibly difficult to enter the realm of heaven and the will of God through institutions and forms. Those who do not believe can easily enter because they do not know, but to remove the entanglements of theories and criticisms... It is much harder to enter the will of God than to go from hell to heaven. However, those who do not believe...

From that perspective, it cannot be helped to call them a brood of vipers. When you see this, regardless of face or reputation, he denied everyone, from his mother to his teacher to every authority. They were all unclean. Even if they opposed him... it is better to die than to sympathize with them. He died in a position where he could show compassion for them while dying in a transcendent place.

Establish a tradition that can overcome all historical mistakes
Now, why did these historical figures walk such paths? You must understand that they walked those paths to inherit a past that is right for God, to establish a past. When you realize that there were failures in the Old Testament and failures in the New Testament, you must become someone who can comply more than anyone from the Old Testament.

In walking the path of the will, even if it is tedious like Noah for 120 years, even if the path of suffering is long, you must say, "That is the natural path. The path I am seeking is towards a place of invaluable worth that cannot be exchanged for the suffering Noah endured for 120 years, so it is only natural to walk this path." You must discover a natural self that can justify this. This is the problem.

When Abraham sacrificed his child, it was not a problem compared to the noble value of becoming the ancestor of faith who establishes God's will. Our historical ancestors fought to establish a point in the past because they did not have a past that God could recognize.

However, although they made sacrifices, because that did not remain as a correct past, we must understand the historical fact that the providence of restoration could not avoid taking a winding path.
