Similarly, in order for us to achieve this great purpose, you need stimulation. Where will you receive that stimulation? That stimulation can only come through the teacher and then through God. Do you understand? "Yes."

The members of the Unification Church, right? All members of the Unification Church around the world are curious about what the teacher is doing right now. Those who are unclear about that are not members of the Unification Church. They are already lagging behind and are on the other side of the wall. You need stimulation. Do you understand? "Yes." In following the teacher through the teacher's words, you must set the teacher as your standard. If that becomes unclear, you must pray. You must pray and receive guidance in the spiritual aspect to walk the path.

The teacher also walks like that. Among you, there are no people who can stimulate the teacher. Here in the Unification Church, there are members, and there is a president of the association, but I do not discuss all these world-historical issues with the president. No matter how many members there are in America or around the world, I do not consult them.

That is why the position of a parent is a lonely one. Isn’t it? Children may have someone to consult, but parents do not have such children. When you see that, you realize that God is a pitiful being. Who would God consult? Isn’t that right? Without consulting anyone, He decides based on His own possessions, and while He can rejoice and agree with the results of those decisions, there is no way to consult anyone.

That is why Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is an extremely lonely person. He has no friends, no teachers, and no colleagues. I have walked this path alone until now. In the personal restoration process, I fought alone, and in the family restoration process, I took the lead, and in the tribal restoration process, I took the lead, and in the national restoration process, I took the lead, and I am currently leading in the global restoration process. Do you understand? "Yes."

Yet, despite not failing, I have managed to break through this much, which is better than anyone in history. In this process, Noah broke down, Abraham broke down, Moses broke down, John the Baptist broke down, and Jesus also failed, but I have now reached a stage where I can avoid a position where I cannot fulfill my purpose, which is indeed great.

You need to understand that God has been trying for 6,000 years, repeatedly failing, and today has managed to partition this much, forming an expectation that can present a global direction. You need to realize that this is an astonishing fact. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You do not know. That is why you need to be stimulated through the teacher. Other than that, you will be stimulated through God.

You need to know what kind of path Heaven is taking. 
When the teacher sees you working, he agrees and is grateful. However, that does not help me at all in my path of indemnity and restoration. I know that it only adds to my many sorrows and difficulties without providing any help.

That is why I do not trust anyone. Honestly, I do not trust anyone. If my child were to betray this will, they would be my enemy. I would wish that child were dead. Isn’t that harsh? It would be better if they were dead... Even if it is a mother, it is sad, but when it goes against the will, I would rather they did not exist... That is how I feel. That is why, centered on the will, I am a madman if I am a madman, and I am crazy if I am crazy.

I am someone who cannot trust anyone. Why? Because God has been disappointed after believing until now. He has been heartbroken after believing. So, while I hide what I have done, I question how I can pass on what I am supposed to do, but I do not question how I will fulfill my will. I do not question it with you. That is something I have been dealing with until now. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

That is why no matter how much I talk about things you do not know, I am definitely talking about the principle content. What is happening now... You know, on the first day of May, I held a victory ceremony, and if you see that, those who communicate with the spirit world would say, "Ah! Today is the happiest day for Reverend Moon in history." But if you ask, "Why is it a happy day?" I know, but they do not know. They receive the answer that it is a happy day through the spirit world, but when it comes to the question of why, no one knows except Reverend Moon. Do you understand? "Yes." You need to know that you are walking a path towards an unknown world.

Then why must those who communicate with the spirit world recognize that? It is because they have already established an internal organizational form through the heavenly principles and have laid the foundation. Therefore, by revealing it in the spirit world, they come to know. But they do not know why it happened. The only person in the world who can answer why it happened is Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. Those who were praying in the mountains, whatever they were doing...
The ones who dream of eating are all one-sided. I have met countless spiritual leaders, but they all do not know. From that perspective, you must reevaluate Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." A street vendor knows only his goods, right? A melon seller knows only melons, right? Isn't that so? You need to understand that. You must elevate your perspective and recognize the path that heaven is taking. Whenever the time comes, it’s just “Teacher, our Teacher! Our Teacher!” What do you mean by “our”? Is it a pigpen? You must understand that “we” represents the world.

From that perspective, you must innovate your mental attitude anew and realize that you are at a time when you must reorganize this day. Do you understand? You must be aware. You must realize anew. You must enlighten yourself. In determining the direction of the path for tomorrow, there is ultimately no other way than to be stimulated through the Teacher. And there is no other way than to pray earnestly through God. There are only these two paths.

However, you are fortunate because you can consult through the Teacher. You have a leader, but the Teacher has no leader. He is alone, alone. In that sense, you are blessed. And in terms of responsibility, the Teacher bears an important responsibility, right? Therefore, when God looks upon you, He values you more than the Teacher. In that sense... Do you understand? "Yes."

It is a miracle that I have survived this much without dying or failing. How much I have been beaten, ridiculed, imprisoned, and mistreated... Even now, established churches oppose, but let them oppose. That era has already passed. 

I hope you understand that and inherit the correct history of the past. Do you understand? "Yes." If you do not establish the present in such a position, that present will become invalid. Therefore, centered on the purpose and will of God, you must expel Satan and fulfill the mission of restoring the entire satanic world under the standard of heaven on earth before you die.

If you cannot accomplish it before you die, you must achieve it even after death. Because you must come back to this earth and go through thousands or tens of thousands of times more suffering to accomplish this, you must realize that this short life of 70 years or 100 years is a precious time that cannot be exchanged for any amount of money and once passed, will never return.

Therefore, when a teenager reaches their 20s, do not be happy just because you are entering your 20s. When transitioning from your teens to your 20s, worry about whether you have become the person heaven desires. When you reach your 30s, do not mourn the passage of time thinking, “Ah! I have turned thirty.” When you reach your 30s, if you can say that it was a meaningful decade before heaven, that is fulfilling. It is better to be a blessed person than to live boasting as a thirty-year-old among millions.

When you enter your 40s, do not be discouraged thinking that you have spent your time until your 40s for this purpose. When you cross the hill of your 40s, think, “Ah! This is a meaningful forty, I have reached the forty I desired. Until this day, I have lived like this, and when I cross from my 40s to my 50s, I will do such and such things.” You must be able to greet it joyfully.

In your 50s, if you have served for a long time for the purpose, the longer the period of faithfulness, the more fulfillment you will feel, and if you can make new resolutions of hope, then that life will be a blessed life. This is how you should see it. Do you understand? "Yes." There is no need for excuses.

You must go for the world, and to do so, you need friends, so make the Teacher your friend. You must go for the world. Do you understand? "Yes." To go for the world, you need friends, so make the Teacher your friend. Then, go together with the Teacher. If you go together, you will reach your destination. If there comes a day when I cannot go... This purpose is certain, so this goal is unchanging. The original will of God is to achieve the original intention of creating a world without the satanic realm, to establish a heavenly kingdom on earth centered on true brotherhood, true marital traditions, and true children’s traditions, and to prepare family traditions, tribal traditions, national traditions.

However, because this purpose was not achieved, it was extended again to prepare Christianity to inherit the global tradition all at once. When Christianity unites centered on the Lord who is coming, this world can be made into a heavenly kingdom within three years. Christianity has divided into over 400 sects, so it must be unified. Therefore, you must understand why the term Unification Church has emerged.

To unify, a unification plan must be presented, so the Unification Church principles have been proposed in Christianity, pursuing the principles of the unknown world until now. Those principles do not come from human brains. You cannot do it with human brains. This must start from God, allowing God to recognize the past, penetrate the current world, and reach the destination of the future world without violating the principles. Otherwise, you cannot follow the principles that can fulfill God's will, and you must understand that the principles that the Unification Church seeks to present are those principles.

Among them, there is a solemn task of being able to inherit the past, present, and future, so you must walk the path of principles. To walk the path of principles, you must follow all the organizational compliance of the Unification Church. And you must save the nation and go to the world. Because that system is there, we must go that way. Do you understand? "Yes."

So until I return here, perhaps I will stop by during the August vacation period, or if that is not feasible, around the end of December... Now, where will I celebrate the New Year of the third 7-year course? The Teacher is thinking about it. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Where will the start of the third 7-year course be celebrated? I would like to celebrate it in Korea. That is the Teacher's earnest desire. If not, I am considering spending it in the United States. I will know when I pray. I need to know what is happening in Korea...

You must understand how difficult the second 7-year course is. This country is exactly like that, exactly. Now, all fateful assistance is aligned with our church and the world, entering an era where everything is aligned. You must understand that on the day of entering, a path that the world can move toward will be sought. Therefore, you must unite and prepare to celebrate the third 7-year course together with you in Korea. To do that, you must engage in more intense activities than those currently taking place in the United States. You must engage in meaningful activities. That is the Teacher's request. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

<Prayer> I came to this headquarters on April 25, 1974. Now, tomorrow, I must leave Korea and head to the United States via Japan, as a fateful path has been determined. 

Father, I decided to come to Korea to spend the last crossing of the second 7-year course. Having already passed April, I must advance again toward the battlefield of this 1974 year, seeing that there is a heavenly task remaining. I understood that this is the path of destiny that you must take.

No matter how many trials there are, no matter how many storms hit, no matter how many paths of death block me, I know it is the destined path, so I run toward you, Father, in a state of anxiety that no one can believe or hope for. 

I do not hesitate to walk the lonely path that cannot be discussed with anyone again. Because I have followed only you and the place you desire, even if I die a thousand or ten thousand times, I must resolve the path that leaves behind heaven's sorrow, and I think that I must repeatedly vow internally and externally that I will run toward that place, even if my hair turns white.

I know well how lonely you have been as a Father responsible for history and fighting, and if I can comfort your heart and inherit your heart while being in a place lonelier than anyone else on this earth, I know there is no happier place than that. Father, I earnestly hope and wish that you will take responsibility for the path I will take in the future.

Father, during this time of crossing the critical point of the second 7-year course centered on April, I have come to Korea, faced various problems, resolved various matters, and now I am about to leave. Please understand my original heart and my intention to leave lightly, and I earnestly hope and wish that you will bless your remaining children here.

To love you, to serve you, to be your son who fights with only the standard of a red heart, is the heavenly wish and the wish of our good ancestors. When I think of this, I must not leave behind conditions of sorrow before heaven even if I die; I must not die. Please allow each of us to pledge this. Father, I earnestly hope and wish.

Father, please take responsibility for the situation in Korea. When I think of your foolish sons and daughters who have worked hard for this country, I know you must protect this country. Please guide the path of democracy in the future, Father.

I know that the lonely group of unification scattered across the world is now facing storms in this vast wilderness of America, waiting for the day of the Teacher, and I believe they are pledging to advance. Please protect that lonely group, Father. They have different nationalities and ethnicities, but they have fought for the past seven months centered on one standard of heart for you. Now, to cross the hill of this year, I must command the history of fierce, ruthless, and merciless struggles myself. Father, please make me aware of this and expand their hearts of comfort.

Please do not let me become a dropout in the battlefield you have left behind. By newly planting a transnational heart in America, let the American people unite as a nation and step forward on this path. They are fighting believing that there will be such a time, so I earnestly hope and wish that you will fulfill their wishes.

Father, the day after tomorrow, I will have a meeting in Japan, so please allow this meeting to not be in vain. I hope that this gathering will become a holy assembly that serves as a historical base needed for Japan and Asia, and I earnestly ask you to protect and guide it.

No matter who attends, let them be moved by their hearts, feel that heaven is alive, and be able to make new internal and external resolutions, making it a holy assembly that can contribute to the path of purpose for the Japanese people.

Now, please allow this time to solemnly be a time when we pledge before your will. We know well that there is no other way than to follow the Teacher on this earth and to follow you. May this be the driving force of life, the standard of living, and may we become a group that can go directly to the world of purpose and the world of the heavenly kingdom.

I hope that we will inherit the tradition, carry on the era, and be able to inherit the future. I must become a historical fruit and a central figure of the era, and I must be the starting point of a future origin. 

Please let this time be one where we clearly realize the undeniable fact that without being such a being, we cannot inherit the kingdom of heaven and the inheritance of being God's children, and may this be a time to resolve centered on that standard. 

I ask you to fulfill everything according to your will, and I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
